{"answers": ["constitutional right"], "model_answer": "According to the documents provided, the right to property is no longer a fundamental right in India. The 44th Amendment to the Constitution of India in 1978 deleted the right to property from the list of fundamental rights. Instead, it is now a constitutional right that can be challenged in a court of law under Article 226 of the Constitution. The government is required to pay compensation to individuals whose property is acquired for public purposes, and the amount of compensation is determined by the government."}

{"answers": ["An elevator with a counterbalance"], "model_answer": "A real-world application of an Atwood machine is an elevator with a counterbalance, which approximates an ideal Atwood machine. The counterbalance relieves the driving motor from the load of holding the elevator cab, requiring it to overcome only the weight difference and inertia of the two masses. This principle is also used in funicular railways, elevators on the Eiffel Tower, ski lifts, and boat lifts, among other examples."}
